We waited one hour and none really helped, they just asked us to wait a couple of hours more. At 19:00 they asked us to try the water but we were already having dinner. I talked to the manager who barely spoke English and she looked like was her first day at school, she clearly didn't know what to do, she didn't offer any kind of solution or compensation (never happened to me before). How is possible Marriott leaders don't understand how to manage an hotel??? It was the first time in 10 years in China for me to be treated like that. Congratulations you won!

In conclusion, I left the day after and went to Hilton hotel spending just 450rmb with super service, free drop off at the railway station, welcome gift, super nice and clean room and a robot delivering the water to the room. Hot and cool air condition working perfectly. It's not difficult, you just need to know how to do your job!!!

msg:According to my own habit of staying in hotels, I chose the executive room of this hotel after comparison. I stayed for 4 days and 3 nights. I think my original choice was correct.
After arriving at the hotel, because the room had not been cleaned yet, the front desk receptionist warmly greeted my colleagues to take me to the executive lounge to rest for a while and then entered the room. The room is spacious, bright and comfortable, and a plate of fruit was specially sent. The view outside the window is unobstructed, and Wanda Plaza is downstairs.
The room service is very careful and calls to confirm whether it needs to be cleaned. The food delivery service tastes good, and the price is moderate and there is no service charge.
The executive lounge has an elegant environment and is equipped with meeting rooms, computer file printing, etc. Breakfast and dinner are provided every day. Although dinner is a simple meal, the variety is not small. At other times, tea, drinks, fruits and biscuits are provided. It would be better if some small sandwiches or desserts can be provided.
The hotel has a variety of breakfast varieties, with local and other local special snacks, which can meet the needs of different groups of people. Moreover, each table is placed with "empty" or "guest" table signs to avoid embarrassment when there are many people.
In short, I will stay in this hotel again next time I have the opportunity and will actively promote it to my friends.

1. Room facilities
The room style is relatively simple, the facilities are well maintained, and there is basically no obvious damage. However, the room on the 36th floor where I first stayed was quite hot. Note that I used the word hot without exaggeration. When the outdoor temperature was 0¬∞C, the indoor temperature was 26¬∞C with the windows open and the air conditioner turned on. I couldn‚Äôt sleep at all. Fortunately, I got a lot of benefits later good solution
2. Meals
The lounge provides freshly squeezed juices and soft drinks throughout the day, with a wide variety of services. The hot dry noodles and beef noodles for breakfast in the restaurant on the 2nd floor are impressive.
3. Recreation facilities
There is a swimming pool and gymnasium on the 7th floor of the hotel. The swimming pool is of regular size. Fortunately, few people use it.
4. Service
I didn't choose to book with Marriott members for this stay, but the service quality and trea**ent are still very guaranteed. High overall score and most impressive for such a busy hotel.
The first is to mention Wang Hailan, the customer service attendant, who saw that after I used white paper as a mouse pad, I took the initiative to leave a mouse pad when I cleaned the room. I was very surprised to see it when I returned to the room.
The second is Fiona, the waiter in the lounge. When I was dining at hh in the evening, I learned that I needed 3 meals, and actively helped me apply for 3 administrative benefits. The waiters can also actively provide services such as pouring juice, pouring coffee, etc.
The third is to thank a young lady at the front desk of the hotel, who did not write down her name. As mentioned above, the room on the 36th floor of the executive floor was extremely hot at the beginning. Considering the central air-conditioning, changing rooms may not solve the problem. My co-residents and I have basically accepted it. We first asked the hotel to borrow a phone at night. The fan blew wildly. The third night was unbearable, with the mentality of trying it one last time, hoping to at least ease it a little bit anyway. The front desk selected 3 rooms with different floors and different orientations for me in one go, and asked my colleagues to take me to test them one by one. Among them, the room on the 27th floor was very cool. I changed rooms smoothly and slept very well that night.
